Tradução do roteiro de Angelique para Super Famicom
Planilha adicionada em 23/09/2023: Seção Sonhos concluída; a maior parte da seção de Julious e um pouco da abertura. Espero que seja atualizada em breve. Relativamente.

Última atualização deste documento ( 19/05/2021 ): Adicionada seção introdutória; informações sobre o livro concluídas e este documento "concluído" por ora. A seguir, a planilha que relaciona as falas em japonês com as falas em inglês.

----------------

Abertura | Julious | Clavis | Randy | Lumiale | Oscar | Marcel | Zephel | Olivie | Luva | crítica | sonhos | final

----------------

Introdução
O documento a seguir pretende ser uma tradução eventual de... bem, da maior parte do texto do primeiro jogo otome, Angelique . Estou trabalhando com base no roteiro fornecido pelo livro da Koei, Anjeriiku Messeeji Korekushon ( Coleção de Mensagens de Angelique ). Este roteiro tem suas limitações: ele é baseado na versão para Windows 95 da versão expandida do jogo, Angelique Special , e se concentra nas interações da heroína com as Guardiãs — interlúdios como a história de Sara e Pastha e a amizade de Angelique com Rosalia não estão incluídos. No entanto, ainda não encontrei nenhuma diferença entre o texto da versão para Windows e a versão original para Super Famicom (além do texto que acompanha certos eventos adicionados para Special ); obviamente, porém, mais verificações precisarão ser feitas. (Um passo de cada vez, no entanto — traduzir o texto do Windows 95 por si só já é um trabalho enorme.) Quanto às cenas que faltam, a solução mais simples é recorrer a vídeos de gameplay quando eu chegar a essa parte.

Para abordar algumas objeções que certamente serão levantadas de antemão:

- Sim, eu sei que um roteiro em inglês precisaria ser bastante editado para se adequar às limitações de tamanho de uma ROM de Super Famicom.
- Sim, eu sei que esta tradução tem valor limitado para inserção na ROM sem as falas correspondentes em japonês. (Elas serão adicionadas após a conclusão da tradução.)
- Sim, eu sei que é necessário muito mais do que uma tradução de roteiro para que um patch de tradução funcione.

Mas isto é um começo, o que é mais do que existia antes.

Esta tradução adota o formato do livro da Coleção de Mensagens Angélicas , que utiliza fluxogramas para as conversas mantidas com os Guardiões em seus escritórios, no Instituto Real de Pesquisa e na cabana de adivinhação. Para dar um exemplo:

Pergunta ou comentário do Guardião nº 1
└─➝ Primeira opção de resposta da Heroína ao comentário nº 1 do Guardião
   Resposta do Guardião à primeira opção de resposta
└─➝ Segunda opção de resposta da Heroína ao comentário nº 1 do
   Guardião Resposta do Guardião à segunda opção de resposta, que gera uma pergunta adicional
   └─➝ Primeira opção de resposta da Heroína à pergunta adicional
      Comentário do Guardião
   └─➝ Primeira opção de resposta da Heroína à pergunta adicional
      Comentário do Guardião

E assim por diante. O formato do livro poderia ser melhorado para maior clareza no futuro — o uso de recuos poderia ser muito melhor, por exemplo, e meus próprios recuos nos fluxogramas não se ajustam automaticamente — mas terá que servir por enquanto. (Veja bem: se esperarmos que minhas habilidades em HTML do final dos anos 90 otimizem a apresentação, esta tradução jamais será concluída.)

Resumindo: Sim, está um pouco bruto, principalmente na apresentação. Mas este projeto exige muito trabalho. O trabalho será feito, mas será um passo de cada vez.

Se você tiver alguma dúvida ou comentário, fique à vontade para fazê-lo.




Tradução de Angelique Super Famicom

ABERTURA

Dia: Vossa Majestade - então finalmente chegou a hora do seu plano...

Rainha: Sim. Devemos deixar tudo em suas mãos. Este universo... o futuro... e a própria esperança...

Bem, não importa. Afinal, eu vou ser rainha. Agora, vamos abrir essas portas. Lá vamos nós!

Rainha: Angélica, Rosalia... Em nome da Rainha, nomeio vocês duas como candidatas ao trono.
A partir de agora, vocês realizarão um exame para determinar qual de vocês é a mais adequada para governar o universo como Rainha.
É incomum que a próxima Rainha seja escolhida por um método como este... mas suas qualidades singulares despertam grandes esperanças.
Desejo que demonstrem os talentos que possuirão como a próxima Rainha. O exame envolverá os Guardiões que vocês veem aqui, bem como minha vice... Dia.
Permitam-me apresentar a Ajudante da Rainha, Dia. Ela estará à disposição de vocês durante o exame, assim como os poderes dos Guardiões. Guias das estrelas, herdeiras da minha vontade! Imploro que não decepcionem nossas expectativas...

Dia: Meu nome é Dia. Serei sua consultora durante este exame. Se algo não estiver claro, não hesite em perguntar.
Podemos explicar o exame?
└─➝Sim!
   (veja abaixo)
└─➝Não!
   (siga em frente)

Julious: Então permitam-me explicar o método do exame. Cada uma de vocês cultivará um novo mundo criado em um novo universo. Nós, os nove Guardiões, que possuímos os poderes necessários para cultivar este mundo, enviaremos nossos poderes conforme solicitado.
Aquela que os utilizar com maior sabedoria e cumprir primeiro os requisitos do exame... aquela que cultivar seu novo mundo mais rapidamente... será nossa próxima Rainha.
Vocês duas entenderam?
└─➝Sim!
   Não decepcionem as expectativas de Sua Majestade.
└─➝Não!
   Então explicarei mais uma vez. O Exame da Rainha consiste em cultivar um novo mundo em um novo cosmos. Nós, os nove Guardiões, possuímos os poderes necessários para cultivar seu mundo e os utilizaremos conforme solicitado. Aquela que os utilizar com maior sabedoria e cumprir primeiro os requisitos do exame... aquela que cultivar seu novo mundo mais rapidamente... será nossa próxima Rainha.

Dia: Aqui estamos, nos céus acima do seu planeta, no novo universo. O Exame da Rainha acontecerá aqui.

Quando uma de vocês liderar seu povo desde os confins do continente até a ilha central, o exame terminará.

Rosalia, este é o continente que você irá cultivar. Escolha um nome para sua terra e encontre seu sumo sacerdote...

   (Pede explicação)

   Este é o nome que Rosalia deu ao seu continente. Por favor, dê um nome apropriado ao seu continente.

   (Insira um campo em branco)

   └─➝Sim, por favor!
      Bem, então, o que acha de "Elísio"?

Randy: Dia! Wow, you're asking ME to explain something so important...I'm honored! It was "Angelique," right? My name's Randy! I'm the Guardian of Courage-Bearing Wind! So, Angelique - what would you like me to explain?

-> "Lend me your power!"

Randy: First, let me explain about our powers! I'll leave conversation to the guys who're better at it. Cultivation will send my power to Elysium. Obstruction returns power sent to Felicia back to me! When you submit a request, you have to choose to cultivate or obstruct. So I'll ask you: what do you want to use my power to do?

-> Cultivate!

Randy: How much power I send to Elysium is determined by how much of YOUR power you want to use. If you want to send a lot of power to Elysium, it'll cost you 4 units of your power; if you just wanna send a little, it'll cost you 2. How much power do you want to send right now?

-> A little

Randy: Cultivate a little? I'll be sure to remember your request! Leave it to me! ...Well, that's what I'd usually say, anyway. You can change your requests the same day you make them, by the way. Be careful, though - you won't get the power you spent for your first request back! You gotta think carefully about how much power you have left and use your requests efficiently - that's the trick to cultivation!
Mm. Well, do your best starting next Monday, Angelique!

Angelique: Thanks, Randy! I will!

Angelique: Pleased to meet you, Clavis!

Clavis: ...Mm. Allow me to tell you something to your advantage. I believe this is written in your student handbook, but the B button is cancel. You can use it to withdraw from a wide array of situations - to cancel a request without spending power, for instance. If you are presented with two choices and are at a loss for an answer, you can press B to select "I don't care." If your two choices are "yes" or "no," however...pressing B will select "no." The B button can be convenient, but use it carefully. ...Ahh, speaking of the B button: you can also use it to interrupt others and cut them off. ...That is quite useful. ...That may have been a difficult conversation for you, Angelique. Well, then... Do your best.

-> Myself

Lumiale: In this manner, you will choose a subject, and I will then ask your thoughts on it. We are a collection of rather strong personalities...if I may say so myself. However, I believe conversation to be important, as it allows you to understand another's thoughts and become closer to them!

Therefore, here, you can research how much of our power your land requires. If you so desire, you may also obtain more detailed data - but it will require one unit of your power to do so. Come here starting this Monday, when you will be able to use your power, and ask the Guardian you meet.

But, you know, Angelique...if you're HERE, perhaps you're piqued about...personal relationships? If that's the case, try talking to the Guardian here! He'll be sure to help you out! I know *I* will~ If you want to get along better with someone, say "I want my relationships to improve" - and tell him with *who.* If you want the GUARDIAN to get along better with someone, say, "I want your relationships to improve," and name the other party. What happens next depends on the feelings of the two people involved. If all goes well, their affinity will go up! Long story short, it'll work just like one of Sara's charms. You need just 1 unit of power! Now, then, Angelique: look sharp, think smart...and MAYBE you'll find the right path. Or maybe not!

-> WHAT?

Date Invitation

*Gladly! (common)
*Common*

a. Anywhere is fine

B. Well, then, let us stay and chat here.

*I'm sorry...
*Weekday: made a date*
Angelique. Our date was for Sunday, but shall we change it to today?
-> Refuse
But I thought you had time to spare on your schedule... Oh, well. We shall see each other on Sunday.
*Weekday: no date*
Angelique. Shall we spend some time together today?
-> I'm sorry
You must be quite engrossed in cultivating your continent to refuse an intivation from me. I will be looking forward to the results!
*Saturday: made a date*
We had made a date for tomorrow, but other business might interfere. I could accompany you today, if it would be convenient.
-> Refuse
Then it can't be helped. We will have to call things off for today. See that you have your schedule open next time. Are we agreed?
*Saturday: no date*
Angelique. I realize that today is Saturday, but if it is acceptable to you, I would not mind accompanying you somewhere.
-> Refuse
I see. You seem to understand that your duties as a Queen Candidate take priority.
*Sunday: made a date*
Angelique. I had made a date with you today.
-> Refuse
Angelique. To renege once you have made a promise is quite unbecoming to a Queen Candidate.
*Sunday: no date*
Angelique. I have some free time today - as do you, I see. I would not mind going somewhere.
-> Refuse
Angelique. I am a busy man. I do not know when I might next have time to spare on my schedule!

On a Date

...What shall we discuss?
* Your favorite things
A. When it comes to coffee, I naturally insist on espresso. The harmony of its deep flavor with its rich aroma is so pleasing.
B. I am quite fond of terrine. Not only is it flavorful; it is refined as well, and adds a touch of class to any environment. Atmosphere is one of the most important influences on the flavor of cuisine. On that point, terrine has no equal.
* Things you can't stand
A. ...And what will you do with that information? ...Very well; I will answer. Oysters. A single look at an oyster, and I lose my appetite.
B. Things I can't stand...and what will you do with that information? ...Very well; I shall answer. I've no love for such a classless dish as fried rice. So oily - I can't stand it.
*Your ideal woman
You wish to know that?... Very well; I shall answer. In a few words, she would possess a combination of beauty, kindness, and wisdom. ...I don't know why I am talking to you of such things. Let us end this conversation here.
*A problematic woman
There is no type of woman in particular that poses a problem for me...but I just can't enamor myself of ill-mannered women. Why? Because that boorishness so often wounds others emotionally. You - and even I myself - should reflect on if we have unintentionally caused the feelings of others to be hurt.
*Your hobbies
A. I have an interest in horseback riding. Making a horse run as if dancing with grace and beauty at my command: the pleasure it gives me is difficult to put into words.
B. Chess. Reading your opponent's movements, considering your best move...I find it quite fascinating. The game might hold some valuable lessons for you that could be of use in the Queen's examination.
*Your homeland
I was born on the main planet, the center of this world. I received gifted education there starting in my early youth. My family, you see, had produced many guardians previously. I had thought it harsh, but now, I understand the love that was showered upon me. ...At times, love is something given harshly. You would do well to remember that.
*Personal matters
A. I am said to be hard on others, but I am even harder on myself - which is only natural for one in a position of leadership.
B. Personal matters? That information will not assist you in becoming Queen. Therefore, I have no reason to answer.

*Your viewpoints
On what subject would you like my opinion?
*Concern for my planet
A. The people of Elysium all live their lives to the fullest. Their fate is in your hands alone. I want you to do your best - not only as a Queen Candidate, but as the one who controls their destinies.
B. I, too, hold the average Guardian's regard for the people of Elysium. But that is all; I have no particular affection for them.
C. That land is for you to cultivate. My thoughts are immaterial.
*The Queen's examination
A. The Queen is the only one who can lead the people of this world - and, even though it was not your will, you were chosen as a candidate for that position. I do not yet know whether or not you will be chosen as Queen. However, you were recognized to hold that potential - so I want you to make the most of it for the sake of the future of this world.
B. You are a Queen Candidate. That privilege is not extended to just anyone. Take heart in that fact! It is difficult, I suppose, but do your best. That is all I can tell you.
C. ...Someone must become the Queen - just as someone must fill the post of Guardian. You should know that as well as I.
*Do you enjoy your job?
A. I assist a Queen who bears the world upon her shoulders. There is no job more fulfilling. As a Queen Candidate, I hope you feel even more strongly than I toward your duty.
B. Whether I like or dislike my job matters not. I see it as my duty - the duty entrusted to the one who possesses the power of the Guardian of Light.
C. It is my job. There is no need for me to say whether or not I enjoy it.
*Feelings about your fellow Guardians
A. A strange question to ask. We have our differences of opinion at times, but that is only because we all wish to make the world a better place. We band together as Guardians to support the Queen. And so, to me, they are all trustworthy comrades.
B. Well, there are those in whom I can place my confidence, and those I cannot - unavoidable, I suppose, in a group of nine. You, too, should do your best to train your eyes and become a keen judge of character.
C. I cannot rely upon the other Guardians. That is why I must exhaust myself so. From my perspective, the others do not appear to be attempting to fulfill their duties.
*Do you like going outside?
A. Yes, I do indeed like going outside! Is that surprising? I find it pleasantly refreshing to do so. When I go outside, I can see and hear so much, and I can learn the ideas of many others. That is extremely important to me!
B. I find it pleasing to go outside on occasion, for a change of pace. Take care, though, not to overindulge in the habit - for your people have only you on whom to rely!
C. I am not fond of going outside. You as well - if you have the time to go outside, you should spend it instead on cultivation.
*Do you like talking?
A. I am fond of conversing with others. Doing so enables you to learn how your viewpoints differ from theirs. To approach it from the opposite direction, hearing viewpoints unlike yours brings your own opinions more sharply into focus. In other words, by better acquainting yourself with the other person, you gain a better understanding of yourself. Yes - I believe that conversing with others is an important part of self-improvement.
B. I recognize that it is important to speak with others to know them better and to have them know you. I am not, however, fond of idle chit-chat.
C. I am not greatly fond of it. Debate is fine, though conversation rarely consists of that. It is simply wasted time.

That is all I have to say in response. Does this satisfy you? Then I will take my leave.

On a Date

I see... What shall we discuss?
* Your favorite things
A. I am for some reason fond of food with a pleasant aroma. As for beverages, I prefer herbal teas. Were you aware that there are herbs capable of calming the soul or lifting one's spirits? I personally recommend chamomile tea. It is said to invite pleasant dreams.
B. My favorite things...might you refer to food? For me, taste does not consist merely of flavor; I believe that color, form, and aroma are also important. Creating a balance between these elements might be called an art form in itself. ...Ahh, but we were discussing my favorite foods, correct? Then, I prefer dishes that have a pleasant appearance and aroma...an herb salad, for example.
* Things you can't stand
A. Items I dislike...as for foods, I find it difficult to enjoy turkey. I have no objections to the taste itself, but...well, when the bird itself is brought to the table, I find the sight just...unappetizing.
B. A food that I hate...or would prefer not to eat, perhaps, is foie gras. I believe that once one discovers the method of its preparation, it is only natural that one would be opposed to eating it.
*Your ideal woman
Let me see... A considerate person. No matter how pleasing his or her outward appearance, I could never call an inconsiderate individual truly beautiful.
*A problematic woman
I see... I dislike the company of an arrogant woman. My feelings on this subject are not limited to women; I believe that arrogance has no benefits for you yourself or those around you. But you seem free of such attitudes, Angelique.
*Your hobbies
A. Painting, I suppose. On the planet where I was raised, we all painted and played music on a daily basis. Since coming here, however, I have not had many opportunities to do either. It makes me sad.
B. Playing the harp for others, I suppose. I have always been partial to music, and the thought of lifting an audience's spirits with the sound of my harp brings me even greater joy.
*Your homeland
Most of my home planet is covered by the sea. It was a warm, inviting planet - a wonderful place to live! The people of my planet all adored the arts and prized a kind and loving heart above all else. Perhaps being raised on such a world had no small part in my becoming the Guardian of Water.
*Personal matters
A. Do you not find that simply being near water calms your heart? ...Take the park fountain or the forest lake, for instance. I feel that the sound of the rushing water and the light glistening on its surface bring me in touch with the gentleness and clarity that form the essence of water. It is perhaps the small places like this that are the true source of the Guardians' power.
B. As you know, the power of Water that I wield brings gentleness to the people. Yes - just as water quenches parched throats, so does it soothe parched hearts and fill people with peace. The Guardians' powers and the gifts they bestow all have hidden meanings such as this. It is a most interesting topic upon which to reflect.

*Your viewpoints
On what subject would you like to hear me speak?
*Concern for my planet
A. I as well hold extraordinary interest in Elysium. There is no greater joy for me than sending my power to bring its people happiness.
B. Yes. I do not wish to be actively involved in its development, but I hold an interest in its progress.
C. Elysium... I have nothing to say on that subject.
*The Queen's examination
A. Both of you have my heartfelt support. I believe that either of you would make a splendid Queen. Do your very best.
B. Queen Candidates are specially chosen. I do not believe it is necessary for me to say anything more, but if I must...if you wish to become the Queen, it is perhaps necessary to give a commensurate effort. Your future is in your hands...
C. It is perhaps only natural for you to prize becoming the Queen above all else. You must take care, however, not to lose sight of what is most important to you yourself...
*Do you enjoy your job?
A. Yes. If I am able to gladden others' hearts through the use of my power, than that gladdens my heart as well.
B. Once I was chosen to be Guardian of Water, I could only resolve to do fulfill my duties as best I could. I believe it is not for me to say if I like or dislike the position.
C. Once I was chosen, I took it as my duty to fulfill my role as Guardian...but there are many aspects of my position of which I am not fond.
*Feelings about your fellow Guardians
A. Yes, I find them all to be fine people. I believe our relationships are built on understanding and trust.
B. As you can imagine, there are many different types of people to be found among the Guardians. I cannot be indifferent to my fellow Guardians, so I attempt to keep in contact with them as much as possible.
C. To be honest, I am somewhat disappointed with the other Guardians. They seem incapable of acting with sympathy and consideration toward others.
*Do you like going outside?
A. Yes, I do! The fresh air calms and soothes me.
B. Yes; I do not mind going outside and taking a nice, leisurely stroll from time to time. Doing so revives my spirits as well.
C. If pressed, I would say I prefer to stay inside.
*Do you like talking?
A. Yes, I do! Conversations with familiar faces nourish the soul.
B. I do not dislike it! It depends, however, on the individual.
C. Well... It would be nice if words could convey all that the heart has to say...but that is not the case, is it?

...That is all I have to say at the moment. Will that suffice? Well, then, Angelique, I shall take my leave. If you'll excuse me.

On a Date

Well, then! What shall we discuss? Ask me anything~
* Your favorite things
A. Hm hm! Angelique, have you ever eaten durian? I'd have to say, the experience is...well - it's an *experience*! I just LOVE tropical fruit, and I just *happened* to get my hands on one... Hm? How WAS it? Ha ha ha! Well, you'll just have to try one for yourself! But don't come crying to me~

*Things you can't stand

*Your ideal woman
A cute girl, I guess? But you know, cuteness is more than skin-deep. It's the whole package - the way you act, the way you talk, your *mystique*... I'm really partial to girls like that.
*A problematic woman
Girls are basically ALL cute, but some of them...well, you just can't find a way to it. It's not how they look - it's how they FEEL! Super-selfish, or always gloomy...you know. I can deal with a TOUCH of that, but it gets you down when it's ALL the time.
*Your hobbies
A. It's written all over my face, isn't it? *Make*-*up.* From the tips of my hair to the tips of my nails - nothing gets past *me.* It's more than a hobby - it's a way of life! Say, Angelique - would you mind if I had a crack at you? I know I'll just make you SHINE.
B. MUSIC! I guess. I love both listening to it and playing it. Some people specialize in, say, the harp, but I'M a virtuoso! I can play anything - after my own fashion. I just love playing what I like the way I want, you know! I guess THAT's my hobby?
*Your homeland
Hm hm hm - it's a SECRET. Just kidding! It was - well...the sticks. Far away from the main planet, so COLD - in the middle of NOWHERE, and BORING. So I thought, "well, this is not the place for ME" - and flew right out of there! But y'know - after so long, I actually have fond memories of the place? Ah - but keep this between US, all right?

C. Hmm? Sorry, but - not interested!

4) Congratulations, Your New Majesty. Your bright smile was always a source of endless joy for me during the exam. I will take great pleasure in serving at your side and fulfilling my duties as the Guardian of Water.

Oscar:

1) So the little lady became our new Queen... Your royal charm hasn't escaped my eye, either, little lady. Your New Majesty! I, Oscar, Guardian of Fire, pledge my heart to your service...to the very last of my strength.

2) Congratulations on your coronation, Your Majesty. I, Oscar of Fire, swear my eternal loyalty to you. ...From the very depths of my heart...and with a passion that remains unchanged from your days as a Queen Candidate...

3) Little lady. ...Guess I can't call you that anymore. You saw the people of your continent through and saved the universe, Your Majesty. You are a great woman...with magnificent charm. I, Oscar, Guardian of Fire, pledge my blade and my soul wholeheartedly to your service...Your New Majesty.

4) Little lady! ...Can't call you that anymore, can I? Pity. ...Looks like you've developed those feminine wiles of yours, little lady! I almost want to take you away from all this! Hm. Oops. ...Forget I said that. That time is over! From this day, I pledge my blade and soul to your service!

Marcel:

1) Angelique! Umm, guess I have to call you Your Majesty now, huh! It kinda feels weird - but, I mean, you worked really hard and got to be Queen, right!? As Guardian of Green, I'll do my best, too - Your New Majesty!

2) Angelique...you really became Queen, didn't you? I felt like I really went through a lot, but now, I really want to congratulate you! So congratulations on your coronation, Your New Majesty!

3) Congratulations, Angelique! You really did great on the exam! I'll never forget what happened on the Floating City! ...And I'll do my best, too - Your New Majesty!

4) Angelique. So you really did become Queen. I...you know, I really...um, never mind. I'll do my best, too - just like the previous Queen...and the new one!

Zephel:

1) Hey...Angelique, congratulations. You did awesome! Like I'd expect anything else. You even make me wanna pitch in for once! Your Majesty...I'll do everything I can to help you out!

2) I just...I feel like you used me, really. ...But you got yourself the throne, didn't ya? Tuh - what can I do! I got your back, Queen Angelique!

3) Angelique. You did awesome, you know? I mean, like I'd expect anything else. You got yourself the throne, right? I'll do anything I can to help you...Your Majesty. Now...and forever. It's like I said before, right? You're a really great girl. It's still true!

4) So...you became Queen. Angelique. There's so much I wanna say to ya...but, well. Can't be helped. Your New Majesty. I'll do everything I can to help you out. ...Got that?!

Olivie:

1) Congrats, Angelique! Well, TRY to be happy - and don't think too much about all that DUTY and RESPONSIBILITY that lies ahead~ I MEAN - a mopey Queen can't lead her people anywhere pleasant, can she?! Right - Your New Majesty?!

2) Oh, NO - you really DID become Queen! How COULD you!? --Well, do your best! Don't knock yourself out! ...I mean it, you know. Let's be clear: I really did love you. ...So SMILE, Angelique! That's when you're at your very best! ...And your most adorable! OK?

3) Your New Majesty. The throne suits you. Was I right or what? Life's got tons in store for you! You're going to be a REAL Queen from now on - but don't take it too hard! Be a happy, *cute* Queen - for the sake of everyone in the universe! OK? I'll be here to help you out, too!

4) Congrats, Your New Majesty! All the best and most ~beautiful~ dreams to you! ...But from the Guardian of Dream - not Olivie. OK? Looking forward to working with you, Your New Majesty!

Luva:

1) Congratulations, Your New Majesty! To be honest, during the exam, I was a little worried - but I know everything will be all right with you as Queen! Do your best, and never forget your sunshine and good cheer. Of course, I'll do everything in my power to help you - Your New Majesty!

2) Ahh, Angelique... Um, I...I don't know what to say... ...I could think of no greater happiness than if you could continue, always, to shine. So, please - stay bright, and happy. ...A joyful Queen will bring joy to the universe.

3) Angelique... Please...never forget your days as a Queen Candidate. You're so bright, you're dazzling. ...Your New Majesty. As Guardian of Earth, you have my heartfelt support.

4) Angelique. I just know you'll make a splendid Queen. But, at times, you may face a rough road. When that happens, stop and take a look around you. I...we all will always be at your side, as Guardians, to support Your Majesty...and the world.

---

Clavis: We Guardians all pledge our loyalty to our new Queen, Angelique...

Julious: Eternal glory to our new Queen, Angelique, ruler of two worlds!

And so, a new Queen was born - the 256th Queen of an old world, and the first of a new one. Queen Angelique, coronated in the first year of the New Universe, on day X of the exam.
